      CHPWHLoopTankCompCnt      Number of central HPWH loop tank heaters/compressors          Integer       -  -  -    -  -  -  -  -  -  -  -   Optional input     
      CHPWHLoopTankVol          Central HPWH loop tank total volume (across all tanks)        Float         -  -  -   Units: gal                Optional input     
      CHPWHLoopTankTankCnt      Number of central HPWH loop tank storage tanks                Integer       -  -  -    -  -  -  -  -  -  -  -   Optional input     
      CHPWHLoopTankRVal         Central HPWH storage tank insulation R-value                  Float         -  -  -   Units: F-ft2-h/Btu       Optional input     
      CDServesMBathFix          whether this system serves a fixture in the master bathro...  Integer       -  -  -    -  -  -  -  -  -  -  -   Optional input     
      CDMBathFixDist            Straight-line distance from heater to furthest fixture in...  Float         -  -  -   Units: ft                 Optional input     Error if not:  Value > 0
      CDServesKitFix            whether this system serves a fixture in the kitchen (used...  Integer       -  -  -    -  -  -  -  -  -  -  -   Optional input
